    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer13220370689691829231">Robbie lives in London with his parents. His mother is a recovering alcoholic who one day meets a lovely young woman, Anna, in a nearby park.   <span id="freeText13220370689691829231" style="display:none">Robbie lives in London with his parents. His mother is a recovering alcoholic who one day meets a lovely young woman, Anna, in a nearby park. After a friendly chat, she invites Anna back home for tea and when Robbie comes back from work, he meets her. The two are instantly attracted to each other.<br /><br />Anna is a Swiss national and has been working as an au pair in London, but her contract is shortly to come to an end. The pair are distraught about having to part after only just having found one another, so it is agreed Robbie will visit Anna in Basel, her home town, where she lives with her sister Evelyn and Evelyn's boyfriend, the charming Frenchman, Marcel.<br />After Robbie's first visit to Switzerland it becomes clear to the couple that they cannot bear to be apart and so Robbie arranges to get a job working at a major pharmaceutical company in Basel.<br /><br />But no one can foresee the consequences of this choice; and none of the happy family can know what will eventually happen.<br /><br />A gripping tale of love, companionship and commitment is set against a backdrop of jealous fixation as a colleague of Robbie's forms a dangerous obsession with him.<br /><br />Where will it all lead?</span>

<div id="review_3216451378" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3216451378" />
    <a title="Grady" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1362506-grady"><img alt="Grady" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442472304p2/1362506.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3216451378?book_show_action=true">Mar 03, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Grady" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Grady" href="/user/show/1362506-grady">Grady</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3216451378" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11435194157615619703">A welcome new writing duo!<br/><br/>British co-authors Belinda Vale and Felix Foreman are both single and bond for this very solid first venture into romance and adventure. Belinda is also a poet and painter; Felix has experienced Formula Ford racing and now focuses his interest on unusual cars, observing sports and visiting art galleries. There is magic in their cooperative debut novel.<br/><br/>According to the frontispiece this book is based on a true story…how these two talented writers transform it into an int</span>
  <span id="freeText11435194157615619703" style="display:none">A welcome new writing duo!<br /><br />British co-authors Belinda Vale and Felix Foreman are both single and bond for this very solid first venture into romance and adventure. Belinda is also a poet and painter; Felix has experienced Formula Ford racing and now focuses his interest on unusual cars, observing sports and visiting art galleries. There is magic in their cooperative debut novel.<br /><br />According to the frontispiece this book is based on a true story…how these two talented writers transform it into an intoxicatingly refreshing novel indicates they have a strong future in the literary arena. The quality of prose is at once poetic and a bit raw, using the various language modes within the UK to set the style of communication alight.<br /><br />Opening their story in the year 1988 the first introduce Robbie Munro in a manner that encourages exploration of this primary character: ‘Belting out the latest Shakin’ Stevens number at earsplitting volume, the battered old blue van braked sharply, barely stopping long enough for its passenger to jump out onto the scorching pavement…As the vehicle drove off, leaving a wall of acrid smoke in its wake, the figure – male; mid-twenties, average height – hesitated for a moment, undecided whether to walk straight home or call in his local for a pint. It was a no-brainer really…’ And a trip to the bar unveils his inordinate appearance and the story can begin. <br /><br />In an intricately woven romance cum mystery the plot is developed as follows – ‘Robbie lives in London with his parents. His mother is a recovering alcoholic who one day meets a lovely young woman, Anna, in a nearby park. After a friendly chat, she invites Anna back home for tea and when Robbie comes back from work, he meets her. The two are instantly attracted to each other. Anna is a Swiss national and has been working as an au pair in London, but her contract is shortly to come to an end. The pair are distraught about having to part after only just having found one another, so it is agreed Robbie will visit Anna in Basel, her home town, where she lives with her sister Evelyn and Evelyn's boyfriend, the charming Frenchman, Marcel. After Robbie's first visit to Switzerland it becomes clear to the couple that they cannot bear to be apart and so Robbie arranges to get a job working at a major pharmaceutical company in Basel. But no one can foresee the consequences of this choice; and none of the happy family can know what will eventually happen. A gripping tale of love, companionship and commitment is set against a backdrop of jealous fixation as a colleague of Robbie's forms a dangerous obsession with him. Where will it all lead?’<br /><br />Once started, reading this excellent novel, it is likely the reader will be committed to pressing to the end. This is an exceptionally fine first outing for Belinda and Felix and observing their growth as authors is definitely a journey worth taking!</span>
  <a data-text-id="11435194157615619703" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9115297995116481843">Passionate Intention is not normally the sort of book I would read, but someone recommended it to me so I thought I would give it a try. What starts off as a beautiful love story between Robbie and Anna, morphs into a disturbing and unpredictable thriller. When one of Robbie’s co-workers develops an unhealthy obsession with him, her jealousy and uncontrollable need can lead nowhere good.<br/><br/>Writing duo Vale and Foreman expertly build up a false sense of security in Passionate Intention, before drama</span>
  <span id="freeText9115297995116481843" style="display:none">Passionate Intention is not normally the sort of book I would read, but someone recommended it to me so I thought I would give it a try. What starts off as a beautiful love story between Robbie and Anna, morphs into a disturbing and unpredictable thriller. When one of Robbie’s co-workers develops an unhealthy obsession with him, her jealousy and uncontrollable need can lead nowhere good.<br /><br />Writing duo Vale and Foreman expertly build up a false sense of security in Passionate Intention, before dramatically flipping the switch. The tension is ramped up right until the dramatic conclusion. A great read that definitely has a Scandi-thriller feel.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer3501675559765437870">Co-authors of Passionate Intention; Belinda Vale and Felix Foreman, retells a sweet love story that will astonish the reader with its ending. Robbie’s mother, Fiona, meets a sweet girl in the park and brings her home for tea. Anna has just a few weeks left in London before returning to her family in Switzerland. A whirlwind of intrigue and romance dominates what time they have left, enough to know they have to see each other again. <br/> <br/>What I enjoyed about Passionate Intention is the variety of cul</span>
  <span id="freeText3501675559765437870" style="display:none">Co-authors of Passionate Intention; Belinda Vale and Felix Foreman, retells a sweet love story that will astonish the reader with its ending. Robbie’s mother, Fiona, meets a sweet girl in the park and brings her home for tea. Anna has just a few weeks left in London before returning to her family in Switzerland. A whirlwind of intrigue and romance dominates what time they have left, enough to know they have to see each other again. <br /> <br />What I enjoyed about Passionate Intention is the variety of cultures entwined. Belinda Vale and Felix Foreman give a detailed description of the places Robbie and Anna visit as they get to know each other and their nationality. As with all love; it tests their loyalty, there is family drama, and they have to make compromises to be together. They base this book on a true story. Names have been changed, but the places that were visited are real. I highly recommend this book to those who enjoy discovering new places and romance.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3227176224" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16189099011376808651">Passionate Intention by Belinda Vale and Felix Foreman accurately captures the dilemmas of love. Anna and Robbie meet at Robbie's mother's house in London, and they form an instant attraction. Anna being an au pair will soon have to return to Switzerland due her employment contract coming to an end. Robbie follows to visit her, and from there he ends up moving to city of Basel, in order for the couple to be together. But the course of true love never goes smoothly, and this story is no exception</span>
  <span id="freeText16189099011376808651" style="display:none">Passionate Intention by Belinda Vale and Felix Foreman accurately captures the dilemmas of love. Anna and Robbie meet at Robbie's mother's house in London, and they form an instant attraction. Anna being an au pair will soon have to return to Switzerland due her employment contract coming to an end. Robbie follows to visit her, and from there he ends up moving to city of Basel, in order for the couple to be together. But the course of true love never goes smoothly, and this story is no exception. The writing by the author duo of this book is crisp and clean, yet carries the vernacular of the UK making it realistic and approachable. The story itself is emotional and compelling, pulling you in as a reader, wanting to know how the story ends. This is a mesmerizing book with a captivating premise and solidly executed ending. Highly recommend. </span>

<div id="review_3228016700" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3228016700" />
    <a title="Stephen R." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/89281938-stephen-r"><img alt="Stephen R." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1549132945p2/89281938.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3228016700?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stephen R." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stephen R." href="/user/show/89281938-stephen-r">Stephen R.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781784656911" href="/book/show/50712393-passionate-intention">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3228016700" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer892360192064418195">'Passionate Intention' is the first novel from British writing duo Vale and Foreman. They met after Foreman approached Vale to help him write a story he had long had the idea for. This first venture between the pair is a rip-roaring mystery and love story combined. The prose flows so flawlessly that it is no surprise to find that Vale is also a poet. The story is partially autobiographical, with certain incidents in the novel drawing parallels with Foreman's own life.<br/><br/>The book is an amorous tale </span>
  <span id="freeText892360192064418195" style="display:none">'Passionate Intention' is the first novel from British writing duo Vale and Foreman. They met after Foreman approached Vale to help him write a story he had long had the idea for. This first venture between the pair is a rip-roaring mystery and love story combined. The prose flows so flawlessly that it is no surprise to find that Vale is also a poet. The story is partially autobiographical, with certain incidents in the novel drawing parallels with Foreman's own life.<br /><br />The book is an amorous tale with a twist and will be popular with those who enjoy suspense and gripping narratives. The writing of the novel is classy and elegant; it reads beautifully and is littered with descriptions that really help you get to know the characters and their many layers. It is easy to read and impossible to put down; the characters have depth and stay with you long after you have closed the pages. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="892360192064418195" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_51779181'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/51779181-the-threat-below"><img alt="The Threat Below (Brathius History, #1)" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1582687895l/51779181._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jhn2rqq+6yCjrMIqwrwgyo04SWH4yl7oQg+CIqkxMHe0P598EeAiSASHdks1SSoVW2euqTZH0I8ZccSTZHLC7Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('puyz0k9IYZir6birOq+UtdwCCf+5Xmiwj2cjt4s3thOcytoA9Bao8AzCDMrNWp5qCl3uN3fT5tfUGWUGRnREiQ==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
